#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
# Fail if any String/boxed types are compared by identity to detect unchanged values.
# We only check for the known pattern in setters: if (value == this.value)
if grep -R "if (value == this.value)" -n javaparser-core/src/main/java | grep -q "LiteralStringValueExpr"; then
  echo "FAIL: LiteralStringValueExpr still uses identity comparison" >&2
  exit 1
fi
echo "OK: LiteralStringValueExpr no longer uses identity comparison"
SH

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+set -euo pipefail
+# Fail if any String/boxed types are compared by identity to detect unchanged values.
+# We only check for the known pattern in setters: if (value == this.value)
+if grep -R "if (value == this.value)" -n javaparser-core/src/main/java | grep -q "LiteralStringValueExpr"; then
+  echo "FAIL: LiteralStringValueExpr still uses identity comparison" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+echo "OK: LiteralStringValueExpr no longer uses identity comparison"
